import glob
from pprint import pprint

from fastavro import reader

alert = glob.glob("data/ztf_public_20250614/*.avro")[0]

with open(alert, "rb") as f:
    avro_reader = reader(f)
    for record in avro_reader:
        print(type(record))
        # Pretty-print the dictionary
        pprint(record)

So, from above, we want to put objectId, candidate, and coordinates into the database (what BOOM does).

coordinates is a GeoJSON object in MongoDB used for indexing with l and b attributes.
